				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Launches New Slide-in Ranges and Over-the-Range Microwave With Air Fry Max]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-launches-new-slide-in-ranges-and-over-the-range-microwave-with-air-fry-max</link>
				<pubDate>Thu, 16 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15143121/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-Slide-in-Ranges-and-Over-the-Range-Microwave-Air-Fry-Max_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced its new Slide-in Ranges and Over-the-Range Microwave with Air Fry Max, bringing together advanced cooking technologies, premium design and connected experiences to elevate everyday cooking. Available in both electric and gas options, the new Samsung Slide-in Ranges are designed to help consumers prepare healthier meals, achieve consistent cooking results and create […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15143219/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-Slide-in-Ranges-and-Over-the-Range-Microwave-Air-Fry-Max_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics' new Slide-in Ranges and Over-the-Range Microwave with Air Fry Max" class="wp-image-175588" /></figure>



<p>Samsung Electronics today announced its new Slide-in Ranges<sup data-fn="17e3660e-8a37-425f-b10a-557a2e20717f" class="fn"><a href="#17e3660e-8a37-425f-b10a-557a2e20717f" id="17e3660e-8a37-425f-b10a-557a2e20717f-link">1</a></sup> and Over-the-Range Microwave<sup data-fn="58711a09-cb43-45f2-a141-5b021624f5e2" class="fn"><a href="#58711a09-cb43-45f2-a141-5b021624f5e2" id="58711a09-cb43-45f2-a141-5b021624f5e2-link">2</a></sup> with Air Fry Max, bringing together advanced cooking technologies, premium design and connected experiences to elevate everyday cooking. Available in both electric and gas options, the new Samsung Slide-in Ranges are designed to help consumers prepare healthier meals,<sup data-fn="5d0de762-2267-4ef8-8e9a-354f46736e78" class="fn"><a href="#5d0de762-2267-4ef8-8e9a-354f46736e78" id="5d0de762-2267-4ef8-8e9a-354f46736e78-link">3</a></sup> achieve consistent cooking results and create a more refined kitchen environment.</p>



<p>“Consumers today are looking for kitchen appliances that both make cooking easier and complement the way they live and entertain at home,” said Hyoung Min Park, VP and Head of Customer Experience Team for the Digital Appliances (DA) Business at Samsung Electronics. “Whether preparing a quick weekday meal or cooking for family and guests, Samsung’s new Slide-in Ranges and Over-the-Range Microwave with Air Fry Max elevate cooking and make the entire process more seamless.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Crispy, Healthier Cooking Achieved With Greater Ease</strong></h2>



<p>The new Slide-in Ranges make it easier to prepare crispy, delicious meals with less effort — thanks to Air Fry Max. Designed to deliver crisp, golden results in less time<sup data-fn="8ab84c52-1a62-4ea4-8757-d9ad374d0ed2" class="fn"><a href="#8ab84c52-1a62-4ea4-8757-d9ad374d0ed2" id="8ab84c52-1a62-4ea4-8757-d9ad374d0ed2-link">4</a></sup> without preheating, Air Fry Max helps consumers prepare everyday meals with ease. High temperatures and powerful convection fans deliver the crunch and taste consumers love while also helping to reduce cooking time.</p>



<p>Additionally, the ranges feature True Convection for faster, more even baking and Air Sous Vide,<sup data-fn="b279241f-e0ad-44c5-a3d1-8e05d8619d5a" class="fn"><a href="#b279241f-e0ad-44c5-a3d1-8e05d8619d5a" id="b279241f-e0ad-44c5-a3d1-8e05d8619d5a-link">5</a></sup> which uses precise heat and airflow to help lock in flavor and moisture for gourmet cooking results at home.</p>



<p>To accommodate different cooking preferences, Samsung is introducing both electric and gas models of the Slide-in Range. The electric ranges feature a 3.6 kW Express Boil<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" /> cooktop with dual-ring elements that help accommodate a variety of cookware sizes, while the gas models come with a powerful 23 K BTU Dual Power Burner that delivers fast, high-heat cooking for tasks such as sautéing, searing and boiling.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>A More Cohesive Kitchen Aesthetic</strong></h2>



<p>The new Slide-in Ranges combine premium design details with intuitive usability. Featuring the same handle design found on Samsung’s 2026 refrigerator lineup, they help create a cohesive, unified aesthetic throughout the kitchen.</p>



<p>Additionally, Illuminated Precision Knobs for Slide-in Ranges provide clear visual feedback by lighting up when the cooktop is in use, helping consumers instantly see when the cooktop is on. The built-in display is designed to be intuitive and user-friendly, as well, making it easier to view and adjust cooking settings. This results in enhanced usability in the kitchen.</p>



<p>Samsung also brings a premium touch to everyday interactions through its Soft Close Door for Slide-in Ranges. This feature allows the door to close smoothly and quietly, offering a seamless and refined experience in the kitchen. Whether users push the door shut with a foot or close it firmly with one hand, the mechanism softly catches the door and guides it shut. The functionality provided by Soft Close Door is similar to soft-close features found in premium automobiles, bringing elegance and ease to users while they cook.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>More Efficient Cooking With Appliances Designed To Work Together</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung’s new Over-the-Range Microwave with Air Fry Max is designed to complement the Slide-in Ranges both functionally and aesthetically.</p>



<p>With Air Fry Max available on both the microwave and the ranges, consumers can prepare larger meals or cook multiple air-fried dishes at once. The feature delivers crispy, healthier results up to 15% faster,<sup data-fn="9105768b-36ce-464e-b82a-beb4bfa51044" class="fn"><a href="#9105768b-36ce-464e-b82a-beb4bfa51044" id="9105768b-36ce-464e-b82a-beb4bfa51044-link">6</a></sup> while Convection Cooking circulates heat to maintain a consistent temperature throughout the cavity, which helps cook meals faster<sup data-fn="02ae07ea-9d61-4a53-a24d-ef5f39597179" class="fn"><a href="#02ae07ea-9d61-4a53-a24d-ef5f39597179" id="02ae07ea-9d61-4a53-a24d-ef5f39597179-link">7</a></sup> and more evenly.</p>



<p>The Slide-in Range and Over-the-Range Microwave also work together through Auto Connectivity,<sup data-fn="98984277-dae3-438d-b646-24cf32ab5baa" class="fn"><a href="#98984277-dae3-438d-b646-24cf32ab5baa" id="98984277-dae3-438d-b646-24cf32ab5baa-link">8</a></sup> which wirelessly syncs the two appliances for an intuitive and convenient cooking experience. When the cooktop is turned on, for example, the Microwave automatically activates its light and ventilation hood. This helps improve visibility and airflow while reducing the need for manual adjustments.</p>



<p>Furthermore, the Over-the-Range Microwave features a slanted, ergonomic design that provides clear visibility to the cooktop while seamlessly blending in with the rest of the kitchen.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Staying Connected To Cooking With SmartThings</strong></h2>



<p>Both the Slide-in Ranges and Over-the-Range Microwave can be connected through SmartThings.<sup data-fn="cb0c6b3b-1ffb-4eb7-88bd-99ffd7d78cd8" class="fn"><a href="#cb0c6b3b-1ffb-4eb7-88bd-99ffd7d78cd8" id="cb0c6b3b-1ffb-4eb7-88bd-99ffd7d78cd8-link">9</a></sup> This allows consumers to conveniently control, monitor and manage these appliances from their smartphone or with a voice assistant<sup data-fn="11cdce73-8771-44f3-8801-319e00421f1f" class="fn"><a href="#11cdce73-8771-44f3-8801-319e00421f1f" id="11cdce73-8771-44f3-8801-319e00421f1f-link">10</a></sup> — while also helping them discover recipes<sup data-fn="0f3296b4-fa73-4fbd-93ad-436f4ddf0806" class="fn"><a href="#0f3296b4-fa73-4fbd-93ad-436f4ddf0806" id="0f3296b4-fa73-4fbd-93ad-436f4ddf0806-link">11</a></sup> and plan meals more easily<sup data-fn="a9dd3b53-b907-4afb-9102-3920dccfd11e" class="fn"><a href="#a9dd3b53-b907-4afb-9102-3920dccfd11e" id="a9dd3b53-b907-4afb-9102-3920dccfd11e-link">12</a></sup> using SmartThings Food.</p>



<p>The new cooking lineup will begin rolling out across North America in mid-July. Among the lineup, the Slide-in Ranges will also be available in select Latin American markets to follow.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />

																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics is premiering the next chapter of its <a href="https://news.samsung.com/us/samsung-flips-action-sony-pictures-spider-man-brand-new-day/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">recently announced</a> collaboration with Sony Pictures’ “Spider-Man: Brand New Day.” The film is set to be released exclusively in theaters on July 31.</p>



<p>Directed by Emmy-nominated filmmaker, Marvel alum and acclaimed production designer Kasra Farahani, the new campaign video showcases Spider-Man as he fights crime and puts his phone through the wear and tear of superhero life. In the spot, the Fabricator creates a number of devices for Spider-Man built to withstand the pace and unpredictability of life behind the mask. The teaser hints at what’s to come in the next chapter for Samsung Galaxy, while Ned Leeds uses <a href="https://spideytracker.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Spidey Tracker</a> to stay on Spider-Man’s trail. Spider-Man fans should also keep an eye out for a range of exciting Easter eggs hidden throughout the teaser.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio"><div class="wp-block-embed__wrapper">
<iframe title="A brand new shape for a Brand New Day | Samsung" width="500" height="281" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/ZI2WYzMx0ow?feature=oembed" frameborder="0" allow="accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share" referrerpolicy="strict-origin-when-cross-origin" allowfullscreen></iframe>
</div></figure>



<p>Set in Peter Parker’s apartment, the new brand spot tells an original story that blends product innovation with actual clips from Spider-Man: Brand New Day, giving fans a glimpse of the highly anticipated film ahead of its theatrical release on July 31. Today’s creative rollout teases a larger story that will continue during <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/invitation-galaxy-unpacked-july-2026-a-new-shape-unfolds" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Galaxy Unpacked</a> on July 22.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15141717/Samsung-Mobile-Spider-Man-Jacob-Baatlon_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics is premiering the next chapter of its recently announced collaboration with Sony Pictures’ “Spider-Man: Brand New Day.”" class="wp-image-175581" /></figure>



<p><a id="_msocom_1"></a>Earlier this summer, Jacob Batalon, as Ned Leeds, <a href="https://news.samsung.com/us/samsung-flips-action-sony-pictures-spider-man-brand-new-day/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">helped unveil Spidey Tracker</a>, an <a href="http://www.spideytracker.com/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">interactive fan experience</a> powered by Samsung Galaxy. Now, Batalon is joining <a href="https://www.samsung.com/us/explore/brand/meet-your-team-galaxy/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">#TeamGalaxy</a> as the brand’s newest ambassador.</p>



<p>“The Galaxy Z Fold is a perfect match for Ned and the creation of the Spidey Tracker,” said Jacob Batalon. “Getting to use Galaxy Z Fold7 and Galaxy Watch on set was a cool experience and I’m excited to officially join Team Galaxy as a natural extension beyond the movie.”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15141808/Samsung-Mobile-Spider-Man-Jacob-Baatlon_main2.jpg" alt="The teaser hints at what's to come in the next chapter for Samsung Galaxy, while Ned Leeds uses Spidey Tracker to stay on Spider-Man's trail. 				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Introduces Flex Titanium Technology To Advance Foldable Displays]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-introduces-flex-titanium-technology-to-advance-foldable-displays</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 15 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15071833/Samsung-Mobile-Flex-Titanium-Technology-Foldable-Displays_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Mobile]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Releases]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Flex Titanium Technology]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Foldable]]></category>

                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4gxKVnl</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today unveiled new Flex Titanium technology for the next generation of Galaxy foldable devices. Built on seven generations of foldable innovation and engineering expertise, the redesigned display structure utilizes structural and material advancements to deliver a more refined viewing experience with enhanced durability and reduced crease visibility. Made possible thanks to Samsung’s accumulated […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today unveiled new Flex Titanium technology for the next generation of Galaxy foldable devices. Built on seven generations of foldable innovation and engineering expertise, the redesigned display structure utilizes structural and material advancements to deliver a more refined viewing experience with enhanced durability and reduced crease visibility. Made possible thanks to Samsung’s accumulated display know-how, Flex Titanium technology integrates two titanium-based components — a titanium-alloy film and a titanium plate — working together to balance slimness, flexibility and strength within the foldable display structure.</p>



<p>“Samsung’s strength in the foldable category comes from connecting user needs with our technologies that deliver tangible benefits in everyday life,” said Sunghoon Moon, EVP and Senior Executive, Mobile R&D Office – H/W, Samsung Electronics. “For the next generation of Galaxy foldables, Samsung is building on years of expertise to bring display innovations into devices that enhance user experiences, anchored by exceptional viewing experiences.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Building on Years of Foldable Experience</strong></h2>



<p>Samsung has played a leading role in advancing mobile display innovation and bringing it to consumers at scale through mobile devices. This legacy includes the widespread adoption of AMOLED displays in 2007 and the evolution of displays into flexible form factors.</p>



<p>Innovative technologies can only reach their full potential and provide meaningful user experiences through continuous refinement in real-world conditions and the foldable category is no exception. Across seven generations of Galaxy foldables, Samsung has listened closely to consumer feedback. This has given the company a deep understanding of what users expect from the category: a larger, more immersive viewing experience with less visible crease — without compromising durability or portability.</p>



<p>To meet these expectations, Samsung had to rethink how foldable displays are constructed by bringing together breakthroughs in technology, materials and mechanical engineering. The result is the latest milestone in foldable display innovation: Flex Titanium technology. By successfully integrating display innovation with device engineering, Samsung will continue to shape the direction of the mobile industry and deliver standout user experiences.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Flex Titanium: Next-Level Viewing</h2>



<p>To create a display that provides an immersive viewing experience while maintaining its ability to withstand everyday use, Samsung took a new approach to structural design. This required a material strong enough to withstand external shock, flexible enough to endure repeated folding and thin enough to fit within a refined device structure. Balancing all three factors was essential to advancing foldable displays — and titanium offered the right mix.</p>



<p>Known for its resilience and strength, titanium has been used in some of the most demanding applications, including satellite antennas and the wheels of a Mars rover. While its strength makes titanium a dependable material, it also presents significant engineering challenges when applied to the thin and flexible structure of a foldable display due to its stiffness. Drawing on its expertise, Samsung has integrated titanium into two key components: a titanium-alloy film and a titanium plate.</p>



<p>The titanium-alloy film is a component that supports the display from within, sitting below the OLED panel. Compared with polymer film, it provides 20 times greater mechanical stiffness. A precision rolling process makes the material exceptionally thin — measuring roughly one-third the thickness of an average human hair — enabling a slimmer display panel.</p>



<p>Below this sits a robust titanium plate, a flexible structure that supports the display module from beneath. It allows tighter bonding with the display module by eliminating air gaps between the module and the adhesive on the plate through advanced hole processing technology. This new structure provides more stable support underneath the display when unfolded while retaining the flexibility needed to accommodate repeated folding.</p>



<p>Furthermore, by integrating a high-resolution architecture and next-generation organic materials, the new display delivers ultra-vivid display resolution while reducing power consumption — delivering a dramatic boost in overall power efficiency.</p>



<p>“By introducing sophisticated micro-patterned holes to the folding section of the titanium plate, we have successfully secured flexibility with robust durability,” said Kyung-Jin Yoo, EVP and Head of Mobile Display Product Development Team, Samsung Display. “Combining high-resolution display architecture with new organic materials that maximize power efficiency, we will further strengthen the competitiveness of next-generation Galaxy foldable devices.”</p>



<p>Together, these advancements enable a strong foldable display that maximizes content immersion on a seamless screen and reduces crease visibility — all while keeping it slim. By balancing strength, flexibility and structural stability, Samsung continues to set the bar for foldable displays.</p>



<p>The new Flex Titanium technology will debut with Samsung’s next-generation Galaxy foldable devices. Further details will be unveiled at <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/invitation-galaxy-unpacked-july-2026-a-new-shape-unfolds" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Galaxy Unpacked</a>.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/15071722/Samsung-Mobile-Flex-Titanium-Technology-Foldable-Displays_Main1.jpg" alt="The picture of Flex Titanium" class="wp-image-175572" /></figure>
]]></content:encoded>

				<pubDate>Tue, 14 Jul 2026 08:21:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/14080715/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-Bespoke-AI-Washer-and-Dryer-PR_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer lineup, designed to meet growing consumer demand for appliances that can reduce everyday effort, help manage energy consumption and integrate seamlessly into connected homes. Combining enhanced AI features, an intuitive Smart Screen experience and SmartThings-enabled energy management, the lineup helps users […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="558" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/14083506/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-Bespoke-AI-Washer-and-Dryer-PR_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer lineup." class="wp-image-175552" /></figure>



<p>Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer lineup,<sup data-fn="fd137fd0-66bc-4f84-9394-b1d21ce411c6" class="fn"><a href="#fd137fd0-66bc-4f84-9394-b1d21ce411c6" id="fd137fd0-66bc-4f84-9394-b1d21ce411c6-link">1</a></sup> designed to meet growing consumer demand for appliances that can reduce everyday effort, help manage energy consumption and integrate seamlessly into connected homes.<sup data-fn="d8793d6c-a96c-45f4-a8be-1a890081c887" class="fn"><a href="#d8793d6c-a96c-45f4-a8be-1a890081c887" id="d8793d6c-a96c-45f4-a8be-1a890081c887-link">2</a></sup> Combining enhanced AI features, an intuitive Smart Screen experience and SmartThings-enabled<sup data-fn="566b7911-e2ab-4c13-8dc4-6e2037cc8c42" class="fn"><a href="#566b7911-e2ab-4c13-8dc4-6e2037cc8c42" id="566b7911-e2ab-4c13-8dc4-6e2037cc8c42-link">3</a></sup> energy management, the lineup helps users manage laundry more conveniently and efficiently.</p>



<p>“As consumers increasingly seek appliances that adapt intelligently to their daily routines, Samsung continues to expand the role of AI across the home,” said Hyoung Min Park, VP and Head of the Customer Experience Team for the Digital Appliances (DA) Business at Samsung Electronics. “In this respect, the new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer lineup delivers a more personalized and convenient laundry experience.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Enhanced AI Features Deliver Intelligent Fabric Care</strong></h2>



<p>The new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer are equipped with Samsung’s latest AI-enhanced laundry cycles, designed to optimize performance across a wider range of fabric types for smaller loads and laundry conditions.</p>



<p>On washers, AI Wash+ expands fabric recognition capabilities to include Outdoor and Denim fabrics in addition to the previously supported fabric types.<sup data-fn="2fd94f49-aadb-4754-b47d-c1615764118e" class="fn"><a href="#2fd94f49-aadb-4754-b47d-c1615764118e" id="2fd94f49-aadb-4754-b47d-c1615764118e-link">4</a></sup> Using multiple sensors, the system detects the weight and five different fabric types, automatically dispenses an appropriate amount of water and detergent, then continuously monitors soil levels during the wash cycle. If needed, it can adjust detergent usage and washing time to help deliver thorough yet efficient cleaning performance.</p>



<p>On dryers, AI Dry+<sup data-fn="9c331a37-fe6d-4b43-a72a-fb139f0b65cb" class="fn"><a href="#9c331a37-fe6d-4b43-a72a-fb139f0b65cb" id="9c331a37-fe6d-4b43-a72a-fb139f0b65cb-link">5</a></sup> analyzes the moisture level and drying temperature of a load while detecting four different fabric types.<sup data-fn="1ff8187e-4e92-4800-88ed-18acec524c69" class="fn"><a href="#1ff8187e-4e92-4800-88ed-18acec524c69" id="1ff8187e-4e92-4800-88ed-18acec524c69-link">6</a></sup> Based on these insights, it automatically adjusts the performance of the Inverter Compressor and Heat Exchanger to optimize drying conditions. By generating the appropriate amount of heat according to the weight and moisture content of each load, AI Dry+ helps reduce energy consumption and drying time by up to 20%.<sup data-fn="fe483396-4527-41f6-b7b3-40d0b1522d9a" class="fn"><a href="#fe483396-4527-41f6-b7b3-40d0b1522d9a" id="fe483396-4527-41f6-b7b3-40d0b1522d9a-link">7</a></sup></p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Smart Screen and Voice Control Simplify Everyday Laundry</strong></h2>



<p>The new lineup enhances everyday convenience with the Smart Screen,<sup data-fn="6b5c482d-6c00-4827-bbca-52997a7700b3" class="fn"><a href="#6b5c482d-6c00-4827-bbca-52997a7700b3" id="6b5c482d-6c00-4827-bbca-52997a7700b3-link">8</a></sup> a 7-inch LCD that serves as an intuitive control center for laundry. The display provides easy access to functions and settings through touchscreen controls, while also personalizing the user experience by remembering usage habits, suggesting cycles<sup data-fn="68eb06b2-68de-44ff-89ec-a161903ebfab" class="fn"><a href="#68eb06b2-68de-44ff-89ec-a161903ebfab" id="68eb06b2-68de-44ff-89ec-a161903ebfab-link">9</a></sup> and delivering timely information. After each cycle, users can access laundry reports through the SmartThings app,<sup data-fn="2d4ea185-d3bb-4207-bc4d-baf215979df3" class="fn"><a href="#2d4ea185-d3bb-4207-bc4d-baf215979df3" id="2d4ea185-d3bb-4207-bc4d-baf215979df3-link">10</a></sup> including insights into energy and water consumption. The lineup also features Samsung’s upgraded Bixby<sup data-fn="bc4c33eb-b8a1-446d-86e8-6fa5d38191db" class="fn"><a href="#bc4c33eb-b8a1-446d-86e8-6fa5d38191db" id="bc4c33eb-b8a1-446d-86e8-6fa5d38191db-link">11</a></sup> voice assistant, which enables users to manage laundry more easily through natural voice interactions. For example, users can ask Bixby to start a preferred cycle, add extra rinsing, check remaining wash time or explain information shown on the screen without touching the controls. Bixby can also provide spoken feedback on information displayed on the screen, making laundry management more accessible and intuitive.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Connected Experiences Support Smarter Energy Management</strong></h2>



<p>Through SmartThings, users can access a range of connected features designed to enhance convenience and support more efficient energy management.</p>



<p>As household energy costs remain a key concern for consumers, the new lineup supports AI Energy Mode<sup data-fn="47a8c62a-109a-4092-8bd5-f36ce51d51d8" class="fn"><a href="#47a8c62a-109a-4092-8bd5-f36ce51d51d8" id="47a8c62a-109a-4092-8bd5-f36ce51d51d8-link">12</a></sup> in SmartThings Energy, which helps users monitor daily, weekly and monthly energy consumption while also providing estimated electricity costs. When compatible cycles are selected,<sup data-fn="e167275f-8fe7-4766-8b4a-a65ba40c7ab6" class="fn"><a href="#e167275f-8fe7-4766-8b4a-a65ba40c7ab6" id="e167275f-8fe7-4766-8b4a-a65ba40c7ab6-link">13</a></sup> AI Energy Mode can reduce energy use by up to 70% by applying AI Ecobubble<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" /> technology<sup data-fn="59b094f5-bbe9-451b-8d72-0a73fbc34471" class="fn"><a href="#59b094f5-bbe9-451b-8d72-0a73fbc34471" id="59b094f5-bbe9-451b-8d72-0a73fbc34471-link">14</a></sup> to wash at lower temperatures and extending cycle time as needed.<sup data-fn="1cbb809c-924f-40b3-9d14-703e768d8d8f" class="fn"><a href="#1cbb809c-924f-40b3-9d14-703e768d8d8f" id="1cbb809c-924f-40b3-9d14-703e768d8d8f-link">15</a></sup> For the dryer, AI Energy Mode helps reduce energy use by up to 20%<sup data-fn="7a1da589-f605-4fb4-ae69-7004fcb9ba62" class="fn"><a href="#7a1da589-f605-4fb4-ae69-7004fcb9ba62" id="7a1da589-f605-4fb4-ae69-7004fcb9ba62-link">16</a></sup> through intelligent optimization of the drying process.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Availability</strong></h2>



<p>The new Bespoke AI Washer delivers large-capacity performance in a 24-inch standard-depth design and is available in capacities ranging from 10.5kg to 13kg, depending on market availability. The matching-design dryer is available in capacities ranging from 9kg to 13kg. The new Bespoke AI Washer and Dryer lineup will be introduced in select markets beginning in July 2026, with availability varying by region and model.</p>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Wins Two Red Dot Award: Design Concept ‘Best of the Best’ Awards]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-wins-two-red-dot-award-design-concept-best-of-the-best-awards</link>
				<pubDate>Tue, 14 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/13170020/Samsung-More-Stories-Red-Dot-Award-Design-Concept_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[More Stories]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Releases]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Red Dot Design Award]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung Home Appliances Accessories]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4wFSjSp</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced that it has earned a total of eight awards, including Red Dot Award: Design Concept Best of the Best honors for Samsung Home Appliances Accessories and Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo, at the Red Dot Design Award. The award-winning concepts are AI-powered designs that understand user contexts and preferences, delivering […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today announced that it has earned a total of eight awards, including Red Dot Award: Design Concept Best of the Best honors for Samsung Home Appliances Accessories<em> </em>and Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo, at the Red Dot Design Award. The award-winning concepts are AI-powered designs that understand user contexts and preferences, delivering more intuitive and personalized experiences while presenting new possibilities for future lifestyles.</p>



<p>“As technology continues to advance, the more important it becomes to understand people,” said Mauro Porcini, President and Chief Design Officer (CDO) of the Device eXperience (DX) Division at Samsung Electronics. “Guided by our Expressive Design approach, we will continue exploring how technology can better understand each individual, adapt naturally to their needs and inspire more personal and meaningful experiences for the future.”</p>



<p>The Red Dot Design Award is widely recognized as one of the world’s top design honors. Established in 1955 and organized by German organization Design Zentrum Nordrhein Westfalen, the award recognizes excellence across three categories: Product Design, Design Concept and Brands & Communication Design. Specifically, Red Dot Award: Design Concept identifies and celebrates design concepts before they become tomorrow’s leading products.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Two Best of the Best Winners in the Design Concept Category</strong></h2>



<p>The advanced concept design for Samsung Home Appliances Accessories<em> </em>helps users naturally recognize the management and disposal methods of consumables based on their color. Some filters for air purifiers and vacuum cleaners are consumables that require periodic replacement; therefore, Samsung applied a color-coding system corresponding to management type so consumers can easily distinguish disposal and management methods.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/13173835/Samsung-More-Stories-Red-Dot-Award-Design-Concept_main1.jpg" alt="The advanced concept design for Samsung Home Appliances Accessories" class="wp-image-175544" /></figure>



<p>With semi-permanent parts categorized as gray, recyclable parts as green and general waste as brown, the system proposes a way to intuitively recognize the correct disposal method without separate explanations.</p>



<p>This concept achieved a triple crown at the Global Design Awards, winning the highest award once again — following the <a href="https://bit.ly/4kQji9f" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">iF Design Award 2026 Gold</a> and the <a href="https://bit.ly/47qnRQB" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">IDEA Design Award 2024 Gold</a>.</p>



<p>The advanced concept Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo is a next-generation kids robot concept that provides personalized experiences for children using AI. Users can create a unique AI character for their child by setting the name, personality and voice. It consists of Dremo, the main robot body used at home, and Minimo, a portable version that ensures connectivity anytime and anywhere. The concept proposes a vision of a futuristic AI companion that grows with the child through interactions tailored to their interests and growth stages.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="562" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/13173721/Samsung-More-Stories-Red-Dot-Award-Design-Concept_main2.jpg" alt="The advanced concept Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo is a next-generation kids robot concept that provides personalized experiences for children using AI." class="wp-image-175543" /></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Six AI-Powered Concepts Recognized as Red Dot Winners for Providing Personalized Future Lifestyles</strong></h2>



<p>Beyond its top honors, six projects dedicated to improving the quality of individual lives through AI have also been honored with significant awards:</p>



<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li><strong>AI Beauty Mirror:</strong> An AI-powered skincare concept that scans users’ faces to analyze skin conditions and recommend personalized skincare solutions.</li>



<li><strong>Panorama UX:</strong> A personalized UX concept that automatically optimizes screen layouts, information presentation and interactions based on user characteristics and real-time contexts.</li>



<li><strong>AI Kitchen:</strong> An AI and robotics-powered kitchen solution concept that reduces the burden of household chores by providing personalized meal recommendations, ingredient management, cooking and dishwashing based on individual data analysis.</li>



<li><strong>Spatial Tab:</strong> A future-ready, glasses-free 3D conversational platform concept that enables realistic interactions and natural eye contact with AI Companions.</li>



<li><strong>AI Home Companion PUCO:</strong> A context-aware AI home companion that delivers assistance and emotional connection by creating personalized spatial experiences through timely projection and subtle non-verbal expressions enabled by its articulated structure.</li>



<li><strong>Fluid AI Design System:</strong> A generative UI concept integrated with AI agents that interprets user interactions and contextual signals in real time to create personalized interfaces tailored to the right time and place.</li>
</ul>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="603" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/14094648/Samsung-More-Stories-Red-Dot-Award-Design-Concept_main3.jpg" alt="An image of Samsung Kids Robot Dremo & Minimo" class="wp-image-175556" /></figure>
]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Advances AI-Powered, Personalized Learning at ISTELive 2026]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-advances-ai-powered-personalized-learning-at-istelive-2026</link>
				<pubDate>Thu, 09 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/08141849/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-ISTELive-2026-Samsung-AMS-Samsung-Education-Portal-Samsung-AI-Assistant_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[TVs & Displays]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Account Management Solution]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Interactive Display]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[ISTELive 2026]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung AI Assistant]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung AMS]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4aCGVhB</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[At ISTELive 2026 in Orlando, Florida, Samsung Electronics showcased how connected classroom technology and artificial intelligence (AI) are helping educators create more engaging and personalized learning experiences. By demonstrating new software innovations for its Android-based Interactive Display portfolio, Samsung highlighted how integrated classroom technologies can help schools improve collaboration, simplify device management and better support […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<ul class="wp-block-list">
<li>Newly introduced education solutions personalize shared Interactive Displays and streamline teaching workflows.</li>



<li>A joint session with Logitech explored how connected classroom technology supports student engagement and active learning.</li>



<li>Interactive Display innovations highlighted expanded AI capabilities designed to support instruction, accessibility and real-time classroom interaction.</li>
</ul>



<p>At ISTELive 2026 in Orlando, Florida, Samsung Electronics showcased how connected classroom technology and artificial intelligence (AI) are helping educators create more engaging and personalized learning experiences. By demonstrating new software innovations for its Android-based Interactive Display portfolio, Samsung highlighted how integrated classroom technologies can help schools improve collaboration, simplify device management and better support diverse learning needs.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/08142020/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-ISTELive-2026-Samsung-AMS-Samsung-Education-Portal-Samsung-AI-Assistant_main1.jpg" alt="Samsung's booth at ISTELive 2026" class="wp-image-175427" /></figure>



<p>Samsung introduced AMS (Account Management Solution) and expanded Samsung AI Assistant capabilities, alongside updates to Samsung Education Portal, to create a more personalized and efficiently managed shared classroom display experience. AMS enables educators to securely sign in to compatible Interactive Displays using a QR code or NFC-enabled ID card, instantly accessing their apps, files and personalized settings on any compatible display across campus, while Samsung Education Portal supports centralized user, device and emergency alert management for IT teams.<sup data-fn="3aae5a25-1b21-4048-8f82-ad386bb443c8" class="fn"><a href="#3aae5a25-1b21-4048-8f82-ad386bb443c8" id="3aae5a25-1b21-4048-8f82-ad386bb443c8-link">1</a></sup></p>



<p>Samsung AI Assistant complements this experience with practical AI tools, including Circle to Search, Live Transcript, AI Summary and AI Quiz, that help teachers quickly find instructional content, generate lesson recaps, create formative assessments and support multilingual learners.<sup data-fn="c19f137a-c683-4ba2-a224-e34c7c04cd79" class="fn"><a href="#c19f137a-c683-4ba2-a224-e34c7c04cd79" id="c19f137a-c683-4ba2-a224-e34c7c04cd79-link">2</a></sup> Together, these solutions empower educators to spend less time managing technology and more time focused on teaching.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="329" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/08142539/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-ISTELive-2026-Samsung-AMS-Samsung-Education-Portal-Samsung-AI-Assistant_main2.jpg" alt="Visitors experienced Samsung AI Assistant features during ISTELive 2026." class="wp-image-175428" /></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Supporting Educators Through Practical AI</strong></h2>



<p>Unsurprisingly, artificial intelligence was one of the most talked-about topics throughout ISTE, with educators expressing strong interest in tools that enhance, not replace, teaching.</p>



<p>During a joint session, Jonathan del Rosario, Head of Product, Display Solutions Division, Samsung Electronics America, and Madeleine Mortimore, Global Education Innovation & Research Lead, Logitech, explored how thoughtfully designed technology can increase classroom engagement while reducing friction for educators.</p>



<p>“The educator remains driving force in the classroom,” said del Rosario. “We design our Interactive Displays to make lesson planning and classroom engagement easier, using AI to help teachers focus more on students while creating richer, more immersive learning experiences.”</p>



<p>The Samsung-Logitech conversation underscored a broader shift toward integrated classroom ecosystems, where hardware, software and pedagogy work together to enable differentiated instruction and sustained student engagement. The discussion also highlighted growing momentum around connected, scalable learning environments, as schools increasingly prioritize unified platforms that extend beyond individual classrooms to support campus-wide collaboration and consistency.</p>



<p>“It’s no longer enough to have a device with an app and call it a day,” said Mortimore. “The right combination of hardware and software enables students to hear and be heard, see and be seen, and interact effectively with both the technology and their peers.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Educators Demo Classroom-Ready Innovation</strong></h2>



<p>Throughout the conference, educators experienced Samsung’s newest AI-powered capabilities firsthand, with many emphasizing their immediate classroom applications.</p>



<p>Tambra Clark, Technology Integration Facilitator at Birmingham City Schools and a Samsung Solve for Tomorrow Top 10 winner, highlighted Samsung AI Assistant’s Circle to Search feature as a significant time saver, allowing teachers to instantly surface credible instructional resources without disrupting the flow of a lesson. Clark also described the Live Transcript, AI Summary and AI Quiz capabilities as transformative classroom tools that simplify lesson reflection and formative assessment.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/08143839/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-ISTELive-2026-Samsung-AMS-Samsung-Education-Portal-Samsung-AI-Assistant_main3.jpg" alt="Educators experienced Samsung's latest AI-powered capabilities firsthand at ISTELive 2026." class="wp-image-175429" /></figure>



<p>“The transcription component is the secret sauce,” said Clark. “It listens to your lesson, creates a summary and even generates a quiz from what you taught. It becomes an incredible reflective tool for teachers while helping identify where students may need additional support.”</p>



<p>Jelena Zivko, Senior Instructional Technology Specialist with Volusia County School District, emphasized how Samsung AMS addresses one of today’s biggest classroom challenges: supporting teachers who regularly move between learning spaces.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/08150725/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-ISTELive-2026-Samsung-AMS-Samsung-Education-Portal-Samsung-AI-Assistant_main4.jpg" alt="The session explored how Samsung's Interactive Display models can address classroom challenges." class="wp-image-175437" /></figure>



<p>“The seamless login experience means teachers can walk into any classroom and immediately have access to their lessons, files and personalized teaching environment,” said Zivko. “It also opens opportunities for substitute teachers, multilingual instruction and extending learning beyond the classroom through summaries and transcripts.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Building Connected Classrooms for the Future</strong></h2>



<p>Beyond new software capabilities, Samsung showcased its expanding Android-based Interactive Display portfolio, including the upcoming WAF-S, WAFX-PS and WAHX-M models. The new lineup introduces Android 16, expanded AI capabilities and, for the first time, a 98-inch Interactive Display designed for larger instructional spaces such as lecture halls and collaborative learning environments.</p>



<p>Samsung’s commitment to advancing classroom technology was also recognized at ISTELive 26, where the <a href="https://www.samsung.com/us/business/smart-signage/interactive-display/75-inch-interactive-display-wafx-p-android-os-sku-lh65wafplgcxza/?modelCode=LH65WAFPLGCXZA&quantity=1" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">WAFX-P</a> Interactive Display received three <em>Tech & Learning</em> Best of Show Awards. The display was honored in the Primary, Secondary and Higher Education categories for its ability to support more engaging, collaborative and accessible learning experiences through AI-powered tools, seamless connectivity and intuitive classroom functionality.</p>

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Launches New Bespoke AI Washer Dryer That Cuts Energy Use While Delivering Smarter Fabric Care]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-launches-new-bespoke-ai-washer-dryer-that-cuts-energy-use-while-delivering-smarter-fabric-care</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 08 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07161826/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-Bespoke-AI-Washer-Dryer_thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Home Appliances]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Press Releases]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Bespoke AI]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Bespoke AI Washer Dryer]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[SmartThings]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4gjMsgK</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer, a two-in-one laundry appliance that delivers Class A energy efficiency through AI Ecobubble™ technology and intelligent fabric care. Featuring Air Wash and AI Wash cycles — along with SmartThings connectivity — the new appliance provides users with a more convenient and personalized […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer,<sup data-fn="35f25d91-01cd-4f88-85e3-ee7665d0f2c8" class="fn"><a href="#35f25d91-01cd-4f88-85e3-ee7665d0f2c8" id="35f25d91-01cd-4f88-85e3-ee7665d0f2c8-link">1</a></sup> a two-in-one laundry appliance that delivers Class A energy efficiency through AI Ecobubble<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" /> technology and intelligent fabric care. Featuring Air Wash and AI Wash cycles — along with SmartThings connectivity — the new appliance provides users with a more convenient and personalized laundry experience.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="563" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07162111/Samsung-Digital-Appliances-New-Bespoke-AI-Washer-Dryer_Main1.jpg" alt="Samsung Electronics today announced the launch of its new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer." class="wp-image-175411" /></figure>



<p>“Consumers increasingly expect laundry appliances to do more than just clean well — they want technology that helps reduce energy consumption without adding complexity to daily life,” said Hyoung Min Park, VP and Head of the Customer Experience Team for the Digital Appliances (DA) Business, Samsung Electronics. “With the new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer, Samsung is taking the next step in providing users with appliances that redefine home living.”</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Enhanced Energy Efficiency</strong></h2>



<p>The new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer meets top-tier energy efficiency ratings in applicable labeling systems in markets where it is available, with select models in European markets exceeding Class A minimum energy efficiency requirements by up to 35 percent.<sup data-fn="135af0cd-fcbb-40e9-861e-b5c56255b0f6" class="fn"><a href="#135af0cd-fcbb-40e9-861e-b5c56255b0f6" id="135af0cd-fcbb-40e9-861e-b5c56255b0f6-link">2</a></sup> The new washer-dryer leverages a combination of advanced technologies, including AI Ecobubble<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />,<sup data-fn="bd950c1d-defe-4a15-b5ac-b702c284bd07" class="fn"><a href="#bd950c1d-defe-4a15-b5ac-b702c284bd07" id="bd950c1d-defe-4a15-b5ac-b702c284bd07-link">3</a></sup> a circulation pump and optimized algorithms. Together, these innovations help reduce energy consumption without compromising cleaning performance.</p>



<p>In particular, AI Ecobubble<img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/2122.png" alt="™" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" /> transforms detergent into bubbles that more quickly penetrate fabrics. The technology improves soil removal by up to 20 percent<sup data-fn="3374cf0d-7518-4fd0-bbf8-cadae6ad07b6" class="fn"><a href="#3374cf0d-7518-4fd0-bbf8-cadae6ad07b6" id="3374cf0d-7518-4fd0-bbf8-cadae6ad07b6-link">4</a></sup> while enabling effective washing at lower temperatures.</p>



<p>Additionally, through AI Energy Mode<sup data-fn="0c038e33-9ab8-4c77-8c38-7d6457e183b8" class="fn"><a href="#0c038e33-9ab8-4c77-8c38-7d6457e183b8" id="0c038e33-9ab8-4c77-8c38-7d6457e183b8-link">5</a></sup> in SmartThings Energy,<sup data-fn="ab29c83d-bcfb-4355-9ebf-febf11e7abb4" class="fn"><a href="#ab29c83d-bcfb-4355-9ebf-febf11e7abb4" id="ab29c83d-bcfb-4355-9ebf-febf11e7abb4-link">6</a></sup> users can monitor energy consumption and estimated electricity costs. When compatible cycles are selected, the feature can reduce energy use by up to 70 percent<sup data-fn="4da54327-064f-440d-9be9-7fe41f702efa" class="fn"><a href="#4da54327-064f-440d-9be9-7fe41f702efa" id="4da54327-064f-440d-9be9-7fe41f702efa-link">7</a></sup> by washing at lower temperatures and adjusting cycle time as needed.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Smarter Fabric Care for Every Load</strong></h2>



<p>The new Bespoke AI Washer Dryer provides specific cycles that help users to care for their laundry in smarter ways.</p>



<p>First, the Air Wash<sup data-fn="d1527e93-62c7-4ce6-9025-b59a034aa50f" class="fn"><a href="#d1527e93-62c7-4ce6-9025-b59a034aa50f" id="d1527e93-62c7-4ce6-9025-b59a034aa50f-link">8</a></sup> cycle refreshes garments and bedding without water or detergent. Once the cycle is selected, it blows super-hot air onto the laundry to freshen fabrics. Through this function, Air Wash offers a convenient way to care for items that do not require a full wash cycle, helping maintain fabric quality over time.</p>



<p>Second, the AI Wash cycle works to make fabric care easier.<sup data-fn="9244ec00-f38e-4801-9291-c57a0793d73f" class="fn"><a href="#9244ec00-f38e-4801-9291-c57a0793d73f" id="9244ec00-f38e-4801-9291-c57a0793d73f-link">9</a></sup> AI Wash automatically senses the weight, softness and soil level of each load, then intelligently dispenses the appropriate amount of water and detergent. It continuously adjusts soak, rinse and spin times to optimize washing performance for thorough yet gentle results. At the same time, the Flex Auto Dispense System automatically dispenses the appropriate amount of detergent and softener for every wash.<sup data-fn="8c22d8ee-2edc-41e7-8053-31bba1bc9412" class="fn"><a href="#8c22d8ee-2edc-41e7-8053-31bba1bc9412" id="8c22d8ee-2edc-41e7-8053-31bba1bc9412-link">10</a></sup></p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Connected Experiences Through SmartThings</strong></h2>



<p>Available on select models,<sup data-fn="cb00a431-343b-410d-aad8-27681f19c80a" class="fn"><a href="#cb00a431-343b-410d-aad8-27681f19c80a" id="cb00a431-343b-410d-aad8-27681f19c80a-link">11</a></sup> AI Control helps simplify laundry management through a more personalized experience. By learning user habits, including frequently used cycles and settings, the system can suggest cycles based on machine learning as well as periodic, weather and seasonal needs.<sup data-fn="0f4376ba-4fe0-41bf-9c30-b22660d5ae41" class="fn"><a href="#0f4376ba-4fe0-41bf-9c30-b22660d5ae41" id="0f4376ba-4fe0-41bf-9c30-b22660d5ae41-link">12</a></sup> Through the SmartThings app, users can also access cycle recommendations, laundry planning features and troubleshooting support.</p>



<p>SmartThings supports Quick Remote<sup data-fn="713249aa-0c63-41c9-a0bc-c19e0a30680a" class="fn"><a href="#713249aa-0c63-41c9-a0bc-c19e0a30680a" id="713249aa-0c63-41c9-a0bc-c19e0a30680a-link">13</a></sup> on compatible Galaxy smartphones, as well.<sup data-fn="94a0abcc-b76e-4515-8642-4a7033d10a35" class="fn"><a href="#94a0abcc-b76e-4515-8642-4a7033d10a35" id="94a0abcc-b76e-4515-8642-4a7033d10a35-link">14</a></sup> When users approach the appliance,<sup data-fn="609681d4-0102-4783-a53c-3df202aa22bf" class="fn"><a href="#609681d4-0102-4783-a53c-3df202aa22bf" id="609681d4-0102-4783-a53c-3df202aa22bf-link">15</a></sup> a Quick Remote interface can automatically appear on the phone,<sup data-fn="40033c6e-dc5a-4c15-8cbc-00c55bf837ca" class="fn"><a href="#40033c6e-dc5a-4c15-8cbc-00c55bf837ca" id="40033c6e-dc5a-4c15-8cbc-00c55bf837ca-link">16</a></sup> providing convenient access to key controls such as power and start/stop<sup data-fn="2b0bb1e8-ecc2-4570-b17c-931790049272" class="fn"><a href="#2b0bb1e8-ecc2-4570-b17c-931790049272" id="2b0bb1e8-ecc2-4570-b17c-931790049272-link">17</a></sup> functions. This enables users to manage laundry more conveniently without needing to locate a separate control interface or open the SmartThings app.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Availability</h2>



<p>The Bespoke AI Washer Dryer is available in capacities ranging from 8kg to 11kg. Starting with select markets, the product will be rolled out globally in a phased manner across additional regions. Availability, specifications and features may vary by region and market.</p>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />

				<title><![CDATA[Samsung Begins Mass Production of PM1763 SSD Optimized for Next-Generation AI Infrastructure]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-begins-mass-production-of-pm1763-ssd-optimized-for-next-generation-ai-infrastructure</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 08 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07104915/Samsung-Semiconductors-Mass-Production-PM1763-SSD_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />

									<description><![CDATA[Samsung Electronics a global leader in advanced memory technology, today announced mass production of PM1763, the company’s PCIe® 6.0-based enterprise solid state drive (SSD) optimized for next-generation AI and HPC server environments. As the volume of data required for AI training and inference continues to grow rapidly, enterprise SSDs (eSSDs) capable of delivering data quickly […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>Samsung Electronics a global leader in advanced memory technology, today announced mass production of PM1763, the company’s PCIe® 6.0-based enterprise solid state drive (SSD) optimized for next-generation AI and HPC server environments.</p>



<p>As the volume of data required for AI training and inference continues to grow rapidly, enterprise SSDs (eSSDs) capable of delivering data quickly and reliably are becoming increasingly essential to AI infrastructure.</p>



<p>Featuring high-speed data transfer and an optimized controller architecture, PM1763 is expected to serve as a key storage solution for high-performance AI platforms.</p>



<p>“Built on industry-leading performance, PM1763 has successfully completed validation for next-generation AI platforms and is well positioned to support evolving AI infrastructure requirements,” said Jangseok Choi, Vice President and Head of Memory Product Planning at Samsung Electronics. “As AI models continue to grow in size and complexity, PM1763 will serve as a key solution that enables customers to efficiently scale memory capacity and optimize AI operations.”</p>



<p>Incorporating Samsung’s 9th-generation V-NAND and a newly developed 4-nanometer (nm) controller, PM1763 significantly improves both performance and power efficiency.</p>



<p>PM1763 is available in 4-terabyte (TB), 8TB and 16TB capacities, with the 16TB configuration delivering industry-leading performance with sequential read and write speeds of up to 28,400 megabytes-per-second (MB/s) and 21,900MB/s, respectively — more than 2 times the performance of its predecessor, PM1753.</p>



<p>This level of performance allows the transfer of a 40-gigabyte (GB) large language model (LLM) in approximately 1.4 seconds, helping minimize data latency between processors and accelerators while improving overall AI processing efficiency.</p>



<p>PM1763 is optimized for liquid-cooled server environments through direct-to-chip (D2C) cooling technology. This enables sustained peak performance even under intensive workloads and extended operating conditions.</p>



<p>Power efficiency is also improved by more than 1.8 times compared to its predecessor, helping reduce overall datacenter operating costs.</p>



<p>To address growing security requirements in AI, Samsung has also strengthened PM1763’s security capabilities. The drive supports post-quantum cryptography (PQC) algorithms designed to protect against future quantum computing threats, as well as TEE Device Interface Security Protocol (TDISP),<sup data-fn="4b75663a-f73b-4572-b75b-eabb3b493ce3" class="fn"><a href="#4b75663a-f73b-4572-b75b-eabb3b493ce3" id="4b75663a-f73b-4572-b75b-eabb3b493ce3-link">1</a></sup> which helps secure data pathways in virtualized environments.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07104441/Samsung-Semiconductors-Mass-Production-PM1763-SSD_Main1.jpg" alt="An image of PM1763 " class="wp-image-175374" /></figure>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07104456/Samsung-Semiconductors-Mass-Production-PM1763-SSD_Main2.jpg" alt="An image of PM1763 " class="wp-image-175375" /></figure>



<hr class="wp-block-separator has-alpha-channel-opacity" />


<ol class="wp-block-footnotes"><li id="4b75663a-f73b-4572-b75b-eabb3b493ce3">Trusted execution environments (TEEs) are secure areas of a processor used to isolated sensitive workloads. <a href="#4b75663a-f73b-4572-b75b-eabb3b493ce3-link" aria-label="Jump to footnote reference 1"><img src="https://s.w.org/images/core/emoji/16.0.1/72x72/21a9.png" alt="↩" class="wp-smiley" style="height: 1em; max-height: 1em;" />︎</a></li></ol>]]></content:encoded>

				<title><![CDATA[[Editorial] AI Doesn’t Need To Outthink You. It Needs To Understand You]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/ai-doesnt-need-to-outthink-you-it-needs-to-understand-you</link>
				<pubDate>Wed, 08 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07171651/Samsung-Mobile-Galaxy-Unpacked-July-2026-TM-Roh-Editorial_Thumb932_FINAL-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[Editorials]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Mobile]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Editorial]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Foldable]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Galaxy AI]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Galaxy Unpacked July 2026]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung Knox]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4ePJzlk</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[History repeats a pattern. The breakthroughs that change everything are rarely the most powerful inventions. They are the moments those inventions reach into daily life. Electricity changed society not with power plants, but when a switch appeared in homes. The internet became ours through the browser. The phone became powerful through the ecosystem of apps […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p>History repeats a pattern. The breakthroughs that change everything are rarely the most powerful inventions. They are the moments those inventions reach into daily life. Electricity changed society not with power plants, but when a switch appeared in homes. The internet became ours through the browser. The phone became powerful through the ecosystem of apps that grew on top of it.</p>



<p>AI will be no different.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Where AI Meets People</h2>



<p>AI is getting smarter faster, and this will continue. But to change how people live, it must answer: where, how and into whose hands does this intelligence reach? This will define AI’s next chapter.</p>



<p>AI no longer merely answers. It is entering an agentic age, taking action on our behalf while the person carries the final decision. But to act for someone, it must first know them.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/07144237/Samsung-Mobile-Galaxy-Unpacked-July-2026-TM-Roh-Editorial_main1.jpg" alt="TM Roh shares his thoughts on AI." class="wp-image-175394" /></figure>



<p>That is why it matters where AI meets people. The entry points are where AI understands a person and builds trust. The best AI experiences will come from the devices that know the user best.</p>



<p>This is what Samsung has spent years building. The phone is closest to us, with us daily. The tablet is where we create and learn. The watch reads signals like sleep and heart rate. The TV and connected home appliances add context from where we live. And new form factors, from foldables to intelligent eyewear, expand where AI meets us. Together, a fuller picture of a person’s needs forms.</p>



<p>These entry points are powerful together. Signals from across devices become timely assistance: sleep tracked by your watch shapes tomorrow’s schedule, with information always available. AI at its best works quietly in the background, bringing these moments into a cohesive experience. That is why we have spent years building an ecosystem not just to reach, but to connect more moments.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">Built on Openness and Trust</h2>



<p>Samsung does not do this alone. The platforms that changed the world were the most open. The web was. So were mobile operating systems. With SmartThings, we brought devices, services and partners into one connected experience, shaping industry open standards. Openness lets the best ideas reach people faster. And we don’t simply layer intelligence on top, but design how AI works at the center so it serves each person in context.</p>



<p>But openness alone is not the goal. The harder task is turning intelligence into something personal and trustworthy. The best intelligence in the world should reach people through their everyday devices. But what makes it personal is understanding the user and keeping that understanding safe. That is our responsibility.</p>



<p> As AI becomes more personal and agentic, trust becomes the foundation. People need to know what AI is doing for them and remain in control.</p>



<p>This is why trust isn’t added at the end. Samsung Knox protects each Galaxy device and now the connections between them. As intelligence moves across devices, protecting what flows between them is crucial. The most personal data stays on the device so people can understand how AI is working and remain in control.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading">The Next Chapter of Galaxy</h2>



<p>That same understanding shapes the devices we build. The more personal and capable AI becomes, the more form matters. As AI helps us with more at once, a screen that flexes and folds expands what is possible. This is what makes foldables special: they fold into your hand or open a larger stage. On this journey, Samsung has continued to make foldables thinner, lighter, stronger and more immersive.</p>



<p> AI is also essential in health. How we sleep, recover and look after ourselves — daily choices add up. A device close to us, like a watch, tracks these signals ensuring a better day.</p>



<p>The upcoming Galaxy Unpacked is where we will show what’s next in bringing all this together: more personal, natural AI experiences on a foundation more partners can build on. The question that opens the next era is not who has the smartest AI, but who understands people best, and turns that understanding into experiences they can trust.</p>



<p>We intend to take this path with openness and responsibility, beginning with the device already in your hand. We open this next chapter together at Galaxy Unpacked.</p>
]]></content:encoded>

					<item>
				<title><![CDATA[[Interview] Art Made for the Senses: Karim Noureldin x Samsung Art Store]]></title>
				<link>https://news.samsung.com/global/interview-art-made-for-the-senses-karim-noureldin-x-samsung-art-store</link>
				<pubDate>Fri, 03 Jul 2026 08:00:00 +0000</pubDate>
								<media:content url="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02184522/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Thumb932-728x410.jpg" medium="image" />
				<dc:creator><![CDATA[Samsung Newsroom]]></dc:creator>
						<category><![CDATA[TVs & Displays]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Art Basel in Basel]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Interview]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung Art Store]]></category>
		<category><![CDATA[Samsung Art TV]]></category>
                <guid isPermaLink="false">https://bit.ly/4at8auX</guid>
									<description><![CDATA[“Space and art, as well as artworks and their built surroundings, are inexorably related to each other.” – Karim Noureldin, contemporary artist Can a work of visual art be experienced as sound? For Karim Noureldin, it can. The Swiss artist creates abstract works that guide the eye across the composition like rhythm in music, revealing […]]]></description>
																<content:encoded><![CDATA[
<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong><em>“Space and art, as well as artworks and their built surroundings, are inexorably related to each other.”</em></strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><em><strong> – Karim Noureldin, contemporary artist</strong></em></p>



<p>Can a work of visual art be experienced as sound? For Karim Noureldin, it can. The Swiss artist creates abstract works that guide the eye across the composition like rhythm in music, revealing new details the longer they are viewed. Noureldin describes this as “a visual sound,” an idea rooted in drawing and reflected across works shaped by line, color, surface and space.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="750" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02180347/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main1.jpg" alt="An image of Karim Noureldin, contemporary artist" class="wp-image-175326" /></figure>



<p>Noureldin’s “Brea” (2025) will be presented to view digitally as part of the new <a href="https://news.samsung.com/global/samsung-art-store-brings-art-basel-to-homes-worldwide-with-new-curated-collection" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Art Basel in Basel 2026 Collection</a>. Available exclusively on Samsung Art Store, the collection presents 24 works by Swiss and Switzerland-based artists represented by eight galleries participating in the fair. “Brea” was chosen for its distinct color palette and use of bold pattern, both central to Noureldin’s broader practice. Samsung Newsroom spoke with Noureldin about drawing, abstraction and what changes when art is experienced at home.</p>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>The Sensory Language of “Brea”</strong></h2>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="614" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/03095117/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main2-1.jpg" alt="“Brea” (2025) reflects Noureldin’s interest in line, color and rhythm, creating what he describes as “a visual sound.” Photo by Finn Curry, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha." class="wp-image-175352" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ “Brea” (2025) reflects Noureldin’s interest in line, color and rhythm, creating what he describes as “a visual sound.” Photo by Finn Curry, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. “Brea” (2025) is part of the Art Basel in Basel 2026 Collection on Samsung Art</strong> <strong>Store. What can you share about the process behind this work?</strong></p>



<p>“Brea” began with the process of drawing as a way to build an imagined space. I created it with pencil because drawing allows me to think, plan, imagine and picture at the same time. I have worked with pencil for a long time and I still see it as one of the most direct ways to begin an idea. The movement of drawing also feels close to writing words by hand.</p>



<p>Working on paper allows me to see a space that is not fully physical yet. I find it easier to create a three-dimensional world in this format than by painting on canvas. This is why drawing has remained so important to me. Its energy has been with me since early in my work as an artist and it is present in “Brea.”</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02180804/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main3.jpg" alt="Noureldin works with colored pencil to build spatial density with repeated lines and shifts in color. Photo by Ariel Huber, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha." class="wp-image-175328" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Noureldin works with colored pencil to build spatial density with repeated lines and shifts in color. Photo by Ariel Huber, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. How do line, surface and structure work together in “Brea”?</strong></p>



<p>In “Brea,” line, structure and surface are not separate elements. They build on each other. The lines create movement, the surfaces create depth and the structure holds these parts together. Through this relationship, the work can begin to feel like a space the viewer enters through their own perception. The author George Stolz has described “Brea” as creating a kind of spatiality through the way its surfaces come together. I think that is close to how I see the work.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="321" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02181446/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main4.jpg" alt="Karim Noureldin’s practice begins with drawing, a medium he describes as a way to think, plan, imagine and picture at the same time. Photo by Ariel Huber, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha." class="wp-image-175329" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Karim Noureldin’s practice begins with drawing, a medium he describes as a way to think, plan, imagine and picture at the same time. Photo by Ariel Huber, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>Defining a Spatial Language </strong></h2>



<p><strong>Q. How has your approach to making art stayed the same over time?</strong></p>



<p>My approach has stayed the same through a steady commitment to the work. I studied fine arts, later served as an associate professor at ECAL/University of Arts and Design Lausanne and have tutored younger Swiss artists. Those experiences shaped how I think about art, but they did not change the reason I make it. I still approach each work with the same motivation and focus I had early on. Being able to make art is something I always dreamed of doing and I continue to do it with dedication and gratitude.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02181711/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main5.jpg" alt="Noureldin’s works speak to each other through line, surface and scale. Photo by Finn Curry, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha." class="wp-image-175330" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Noureldin’s works speak to each other through line, surface and scale. Photo by Finn Curry, courtesy of the artist and von Bartha.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. What connects the different forms you work in?</strong></p>



<p>No matter the form, my work applies the same abstract language and creative process to different media. I often think of each medium as a different instrument. The sound changes, but the composition comes from the same place. The works can appear at a small or large scale, within a specific site or as independent pieces. What connects them is the same attention to line, color, rhythm and space.</p>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. What does abstraction allow you to do?</strong></p>



<p>Abstraction allows for timelessness and universality. It’s not fixed to one subject or moment. It can remain open, so each viewer can meet the work through their own perception.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong><em>“Being able to make art is something I always dreamed of doing and I continue to do it with dedication and gratitude.”</em></strong></p>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. How do you think about the relationship between an artwork and the place where it is seen?</strong></p>



<p>Space and art, as well as artworks and their built surroundings, are inexorably related to each other. Whether a work was created for a specific site, placed within one or simply viewed there, each condition shapes what the work can express and do.</p>



<figure class="wp-block-image size-full"><img loading="lazy" width="1000" height="667" src="https://img.global.news.samsung.com/global/wp-content/uploads/2026/07/02182027/Samsung-TVs-and-Displays-Interview-Karim-Noureldin-Samsung-Art-Store_Main6.jpg" alt="Presented on The Frame at Samsung Art Store’s Art Basel in Basel 2026 exhibition, “Brea” brings Noureldin’s visual language into a digital viewing experience. Courtesy of Samsung Electronics." class="wp-image-175331" /><figcaption class="wp-element-caption">▲ Presented on The Frame at Samsung Art Store’s Art Basel in Basel 2026 exhibition, “Brea” brings Noureldin’s visual language into a digital viewing experience. Courtesy of Samsung Electronics.</figcaption></figure>



<p></p>



<h2 class="wp-block-heading"><strong>How Art Forms Unity Within a Home</strong></h2>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong><em>“When we have art in our homes, it becomes part of one’s daily life.”</em></strong></p>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q.</strong> <strong>What feels meaningful to you about viewers encountering your work at home through Samsung Art TV?</strong></p>



<p>Living with art brings art back to a private and personal space. With Samsung Art TVs, the work moves from the artist’s studio into a home, where it can be experienced daily rather than only during a visit to an institution. It helps keep visual creativity top of mind for everyone, even if they aren’t an artist.</p>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. When an artwork becomes part of the home, what can repeated viewing reveal</strong> <strong>that might not be noticed at first?</strong></p>



<p>When we have art in our homes, it becomes part of one’s daily life and changes with the conditions around it. Different times of day, different lighting shifts or even moods changing each time a piece is viewed. These small details can change the appearance of a work over time, making it a unified element of the home.</p>



<p></p>



<p><strong>Q. Samsung Art Store will introduce your work to some viewers who may not know</strong> <strong>your practice yet. What would you hope they notice first in “Brea”?</strong></p>



<p>I would hope they first notice “Brea” as a visual sound. By that, I mean a composition that can be felt through rhythm and movement much like music can be felt without words. Before trying to define it, I hope they spend time with every element of its structure to understand how it can speak to more than one sense.</p>



<p>Samsung Art Store is an art subscription service available on Samsung Art TVs including The Frame, Micro RGB and Neo QLED, offering more than 5,000 works in 4K resolution from more than 800 partners across 117 countries. As Art Basel’s official display partner, Samsung Electronics offers another way to experience contemporary art beyond the fair through exclusive Samsung Art Store digital collections featuring artists from Art Basel’s Hong Kong, Basel, Paris and Miami Beach editions.</p>



<p>To experience “Brea” and the rest of the Art Basel in Basel 2026 Collection, visit a Samsung Art Store on your compatible Samsung TV today.</p>
]]></content:encoded>
